BADZRA YA TH'A SU KHAm ZHES SO, ,DE NAS SNGAR GSUNGS PA'I YI GE
LNGA POS YOL BA'I NANG DU BCUG NAS 'DI SKAD SMRA BAR BYA'O, ,DE
RING KHYOD DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA THAMS CAD KYI RIGS SU ZHUGS KYIS,
DE NAS NGAS KHYOD LA RDO RJE'I YE SHES

BSKYED PAR BYA STE, YE SHES GANG GIS KHYOD DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA
RNAMS KYI DNGOS GRUB THOB PAR 'GYUR NA DNGOS GRUB GZHAN RNAMS LTA
CI SMOS, ,KHYOD KYIS KYANG 'DI DKYIL 'KHOR MA MTHONG BA'I MDUN DU
SMRA BAR MI BYA STE, KHYOD DAM TSIG NYAMS NA MI RUNG NGO ZHES SO,
,DE NAS MGO BOR RDO RJE BZHAG NAS

'DI SKAD CES BRJOD PAR BYA'O, ,'DI NI KHYOD KYI DAM TSIG RDO RJE
STE, GAL TE KHYOD KYIS 'GA' ZHIG LA SMRAS NA MGO BO 'GEMS PAR
BYED DO, ,AOm RDO RJE SEMS DPA' RANG NYID DENG, ,KHYOD KYI SNYING
LA YANG DAG GNAS, ,GAL TE TSUL 'DI SMRAS NA NI, ,DE MA THAG TU
DRAL TE GSHEGS, ,ZHES

PA 'DI YIS MNA' BYAS TE, TZANDAN DANG GUR KUM LA SOGS PA BSRES

BDUN BZLAS PA, 'DI NI KHYOD KYI DMYAL BA'I CHU, ,DAM TSIG 'DAS NA
SREG PAR BYED, ,DAM TSIG BSRUNGS LAS DNGOS GRUB STER, ,RDO RJE
BDUD RTZI'I CHU
